CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Ingredient (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), category VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Recipe (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), description TEXT);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Food (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), category VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2), quantity INT);</t><s>drop table if exists ingredient;</s>
